 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Alzheimer's is a mental disease, due to which the memory of the patient becomes weak and it affects the functions of the brain
 yah dementia kaa sabase aam prakaar he
 This affects a person's memory, thinking ability, everyday activities
 lekin ek nai study kii report main bataaya gaya he ki green tii or gaajar ke seven se alzimer ke khatre ko kam kiya ja saktaa he
 This study has been done by researchers from the University of Southern California
 centre for dijis control and privansion ke mutabik, aane vaale samay main alzimer beemaari zyada se zyada logon ko apni chapet main le sakati he
 People with Alzheimer's disease are affected by their personality, ability to work, think, remember things
 jarnal of biological chemistry main prakashit study main shodhakartaaon kii team ne 2 compound kii jaanch kii he
 The first is EGCG (EGCG) and the second ferulic acid (FA)
 ijisiji (EGCG) ek tarah kaa antioxident he, jo green tii main bharpoor maatra main paaya jaataa he
 This compound prevents the formation of free radicals in the body, due to which the cells and molecules of the body are saved from damage
 vahiin, pichhali kuch study main bataaya gaya he ki ijisiji (EGCG) compound nae neurons ko surakshit rakhane main madad karata he, jisase yaaddaasht kamjor nahin hoti he
 The second compound is ferulic acid (FA)
 ye compound gaajar, oats or tamaato main paaya jaataa he
 Ferulic acid is also a type of antioxidant
 ye antioxident san bern, jhurriyon samet skin sambandhit kai samasyaon ko dur karne main madad karata he
 This study has been done on mice
 study ke dauraan shodhakartaaon ne alzimer se peedit chuhon ko 4 group main baanta
 The four groups included Alzheimer's-infected mice as well as healthy mice
 in sabhi chuhon ko chaar alag tarah kii diet di gai
 These are: one group was given EGCG (EGCG) and ferulic acid (FA), the second group was given only EGCG (EGCG), the third group was given only ferulic acid (FA) and the fourth group was placebo
 iske baad sabhi chuhon kii jaanch kii gai
 The results revealed that mice given EGCG and ferulic acid (FA) diets performed similarly to healthy mice within 3 months
 study ke mukhya lekhak dow
 Terence Town reported that EGCG and ferulic acid (FA) inhibit the amyloid beta protein from reaching the brain, which is responsible for memory loss
 saath hi ye antioxidents dimag ke tanaav ko kam karne main bhi ahm bhoomika nibhaate hai
